# <a name="changelog-for-microsoft-graph"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-101">Microsoft Graph の変更ログ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-101">Changelog for Microsoft Graph</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-102">この変更ログでは、Microsoft Graph と、v1.0 およびベータ版のエンドポイント Microsoft Graph API の変更内容について説明します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-102">This changelog covers what's changed in Microsoft Graph, including the v1.0 and beta endpoint Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span>

### <a name="remove-deprecated-planner-api"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-416">使用されていない Planner API の削除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-416">Remove Deprecated Planner API</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-603">追加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-603">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-604">v1.0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-604">v1.0</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-605">リソース [contact](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/resources/contact)、[device](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/resources/device)、[event](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/resources/event)、[group](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/resources/group)、[message](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/resources/message)、[organization](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/resources/organization)、[post](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/resources/post)、[user](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/resources/user) の、既存の POST、GET、および ATCH メソッドが、対応するリソース インスタンスにスキーマ拡張機能として保存されているカスタム データの追加、取得、および更新または削除をサポートするようになりました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-605">The existing POST, GET, and PATCH methods of the following resources - now support adding, getting, and updating or deleting custom data stored as schema extensions in the corresponding resource instances.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-606">追加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-606">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-607">v1.0 およびベータ版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-607">v1.0 and beta</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-p107">`$filter` を使用して、拡張機能名など特定の拡張機能プロパティの値と一致する　プロパティを持つリソース インスタンスを検索できるようになりました。詳細については、この[例](https://devx.microsoft-tst.com/en-us/graph/docs/concepts/extensibility_schema_groups#5-get-a-group-and-its-extension-data)を参照してください。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-p107">You can now use `$filter` to look for resource instances with properties that match specific extension property values, such as extension name. |<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-610">変更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-610">Change</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-611">v1.0 およびベータ版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-611">v1.0 and beta</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-612">[スキーマ拡張機能の定義を削除](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/api/schemaextension_delete)しても、その定義に基づいて追加されたカスタム データへのアクセスに影響しなくなりました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-612">[Deleting a schema extension definition](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/api/schemaextension_delete) no longer affects accessing custom data that has been added based on that definition.</span></span> |

| <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-931">追加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-931">Addition</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-932">ベータ版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-932">beta</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-933">**booleanColumn**、**calculatedColumn**、**choiceColumn**、**dateTimeColumn**、**lookupColumn**、**numberColumn**、**personOrGroupColumn**、および **textColumn** リソース型を追加しました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-933">Added the **booleanColumn**, **calculatedColumn**, **choiceColumn**, **dateTimeColumn**, **lookupColumn**, **numberColumn**, **personOrGroupColumn**, and **textColumn** resource types.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-934">**displayName** プロパティを **site** に追加しました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-934">Added the **displayName** property to **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-935">**columns** ナビゲーション プロパティを **site** に追加しました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-935">Added the **columns** navigation property to **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-936">**list** および **listItem** ナビゲーション プロパティを **sharedDriveItem** に追加しました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-936">Added the **list** and **listItem** navigation properties to **sharedDriveItem**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-937">**sharepointIds** プロパティを **list** と **listItem**、および **site** に追加しました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-937">Added the **sharepointIds** property to **list** and **listItem**, and **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="dee4e-938">**columnDefinition** リソース型を追加しました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-938">Added the **columnDefinition** resource type.</span></span>

## <a name="march-2017"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1182">2017 年 3 月</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1182">March 2017</span></span>

### <a name="intune-apis"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1183">Intune API</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1183">Intune APIs</span></span>

### <a name="add-custom-data-to-microsoft-graph-using-open-extensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1559">オープン拡張機能を使用して Microsoft Graph にカスタム データを追加する</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1559">Add custom data to Microsoft Graph using open extensions</span></span>

## <a name="december-2016"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1881">2016 年 12 月</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1881">December 2016</span></span>

### <a name="delta-query"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1882">デルタ クエリ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1882">Delta query</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1883">**変更の種類**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1883">**Change type**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1884">**バージョン**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1884">**Version**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1885">**説明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1885">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-------------|:-----------|:--------------|
|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1886">追加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1886">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1887">ベータ版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1887">Beta</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1888">
  [デルタ クエリ](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/concepts/delta_query_overview)を実行するため、以下のエンティティに新しいデルタ関数が追加されました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1888">A new delta function add to the following entities to perform [delta query](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/concepts/delta_query_overview):</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1889">contact</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1889">contact</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1890">contactFolder</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1890">contactFolder</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1891">event</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1891">event</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1892">group</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1892">group</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1893">mailFolder</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1893">mailFolder</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1894">message</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1894">message</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1895">user</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1895">user</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1896">例については、以下をご覧ください。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1896">See the following for examples:</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1897">
  [グループへの増分の変更を取得する (プレビュー)](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/concepts/delta_query_groups)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1897">[Get incremental changes to groups (preview)](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/concepts/delta_query_groups)</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1898">

This means that you will no longer be able to add an invited user to a group using this API. Instead, use the [add member API](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/api/group_post_members) to add a user to a group.</span></span>|

### <a name="groups"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1989">グループ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1989">Groups</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1990">パブリック プレビューの API により、動的グループ メンバーシップのサポートが追加されました。追加された内容の一部を、次の表に記載します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1990">Added support for dynamic group membership through the public preview API, including the additions listed in the following table.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1991">**変更の種類**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1991">**Change type**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1992">**バージョン**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1992">**Version**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1993">**説明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1993">**Description**</span></span>|
|:--------------|:-----------|:--------------|
|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1994">追加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1994">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1995">ベータ版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1995">Beta</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-1996">グループが動的グループの場合に、このグループのメンバーシップを制御する規則を含む、**membershipRule** プロパティが追加されました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-1996">Added **membershipRule** property contains rules that controls the memberships for this group, if the group is a dynamic group.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2117">**変更の種類**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2117">**Change type**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2118">**バージョン**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2118">**Version**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2119">**説明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2119">**Description**</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2124">追加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2124">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2125">ベータ版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2125">Beta</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2126">Outlook のグローバル アドレス一覧にこのユーザーを含める必要があるかどうかを制御するための **showInAddressList** プロパティが追加されました。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2126">Added **showInAddressList** property to control if the Outlook global address list should contain this user.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2127">追加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2127">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2128">ベータ版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2128">Beta</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2129">**invalidateAllRefreshTokens** サービス アクションが追加されました。これを使って **refreshTokensValidFromDateTime** ユーザー プロパティを現在の日時にリセットすることで、アプリケーションに発行されたすべての更新トークンとセッション トークンが無効になります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2129">Added **invalidateAllRefreshTokens** service action that invalidates all of the user's refresh and session tokens issued to applications, by resetting the **refreshTokensValidFromDateTime** user property to the current date-time.</span></span>|

For details, see [Microsoft Graph: Azure AD Privileged Identity Management Preview APIs available in Beta](http://dev.office.com/blogs/microsoft-graph-azure-ad-privileged-identity-management-apis-beta) and [Azure AD Privileged Identity Management](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/beta/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement_root).</span></span>|

### <a name="mail-folder"></a><span data-ttu-id="dee4e-2428">メール フォルダー</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dee4e-2428">Mail folder</span></span>
